# BODY Tab - Complete Documentation

## ğŸ“± Features Overview

### What happens when user clicks BODY tab?

1. **Tab switches** from FACE/EYES to BODY
2. **Body-specific controls** appear
3. **4 main control sections** displayed
4. **Before/After comparison** available
5. **Reset button** to undo all changes

---

## ğŸ¯ Body Controls Available

### 1. Body Shape (Circular Slider) ğŸ”„
- **Type**: Circular control
- **Default**: -15% (Slimming)
- **Range**: -50% (Fill) to +50% (Slim)
- **Display**: Center icon shows current mode
  - SLIMMING (negative values)
  - NEUTRAL (0%)
  - FILLING (positive values)
- **Color**: Cyan accent
- **Labels**: "FILL" â† â†’ "SLIM"

### 2. Height & Posture ğŸ“

#### Height (Vertical Slider)
- **Type**: Vertical gradient slider
- **Default**: 45%
- **Range**: 0-100%
- **Color**: Cyan gradient (top to bottom)
- **Visual**: Gradient fill from bottom

#### Posture (Preset Buttons)
- **Type**: 3 option buttons
- **Options**:
  1. **OFF** - No posture correction
  2. **SUBTLE** - Gentle correction (default)
  3. **STRONG** - Maximum correction
- **Visual**: Selected button has pink border & background

### 3. Waist & Curves (Dual Center Sliders) ğŸ‘—

#### Waist Slider
- **Type**: Center-position slider
- **Default**: -40%
- **Range**: -50% (Slimmer) to +50% (Fuller)
- **Color**: Pink gradient
- **Visual**: Gradient fills LEFT from center when negative

#### Curves Slider
- **Type**: Center-position slider
- **Default**: +12%
- **Range**: -50% (Less curves) to +50% (More curves)
- **Color**: Purple gradient
- **Visual**: Gradient fills RIGHT from center when positive

### 4. Reset All Changes Button ğŸ”„
- **Type**: Text button
- **Function**: Resets all controls to neutral (0%)
- **Visual**: Pink border with transparent background
- **Text**: "RESET ALL CHANGES"

# EYES Tab - Complete Documentation

## ğŸ“± Features

### What happens when user clicks EYES tab?

1. **Tab switches** from FACE to EYES
2. **Eye-specific controls** appear
3. **All controls are independent** from FACE tab
4. **Before/After viewer** shows eye adjustments in real-time

---

## ğŸ¯ Eye Controls Available

### 1. Eye Brightness (Slider)
- **Default**: 60%
- **Range**: 0-100%
- **Color**: Pink gradient
- **Effect**: Makes eyes brighter and more lively
- **Real-time preview** on slider drag

### 2. Remove Dark Circles (Toggle + Slider)
- **Toggle**: ON by default
- **Intensity**: 40%
- **Color**: Purple gradient
- **Effect**: Removes/reduces dark circles under eyes
- **Shows intensity slider** only when enabled

### 3. Eye Size (Special Slider)
- **Default**: 0% (center position)
- **Range**: -20% to +20%
- **Special Feature**: Center-positioned slider with +/- indicators
- **Warning**: "Use sparingly for natural results"
- **Effect**: Subtle eye enlargement/reduction

### 4. Red-Eye Removal (Toggle)
- **Toggle**: ON by default
- **Color**: Cyan gradient
- **Effect**: Automatically removes red-eye from flash
- **No intensity slider** - works automatically

## ğŸ¨ Features

### âœ… **Fully Configurable** - No Fake Data
All settings are user-controllable through `SplashConfig`:

```dart
SplashConfig(
  appName: 'RETOUNIQ',              // Your app name
  tagline: 'AI PHOTO ENGINE',       // Tagline text
  progressLabel: 'INITIALIZING',    // Progress label
  progressValue: 0.74,              // Progress (0.0 to 1.0)
  showParticles: true,              // Enable/disable particles
  showGlow: true,                   // Enable/disable glow effects
  displayDuration: Duration(seconds: 3),  // Splash duration
  logoVariant: LogoVariant.neuralNetwork, // Logo style
)
```

### ğŸ­ **Two Splash Variants**

1. **Neural Network Variant** (`SplashScreen`)
   - Complex neural network logo with SVG paths
   - "AI PHOTO ENGINE" tagline
   - Full progress bar (6px height)
   - 74% progress display

2. **Geometric Variant** (`SplashVariantScreen`)
   - Large "R" letter with geometric background
   - "PREMIUM PHOTO ENGINE" tagline  
   - Hairline progress bar (1px height)
   - 45% progress display

### ğŸ¯ **User Controls**

Change variant in `main.dart`:

```dart
class _SplashScreenDemoState extends State<SplashScreenDemo> {
  bool _showVariant = false;  // false = First variant, true = Second variant
  
  // ... rest of code
}
```

### ğŸ¨ **Customizable Elements**

**Colors** (`app_config.dart`):
```dart
static const Color primaryColor = Color(0xFFf20d80);     // Pink
static const Color accentCyan = Color(0xFF00f2ff);       // Cyan
static const Color backgroundDark = Color(0xFF0a0508);   // Dark bg
```

**Particles** (`animated_particles.dart`):
- 6 animated floating particles
- Auto-pulses with opacity changes
- Customizable size, position, blur

**Progress Bar** (`progress_bar.dart`):
- Smooth animated fill
- Gradient colors (pink â†’ purple â†’ cyan)
- Percentage display
- Two styles: normal (6px) and hairline (1px)

**Logos**:
- Neural Network: Custom painted paths and nodes
- Geometric: Large "R" with background network pattern

## ğŸš€ How to Use

### 1. Run the app:
```bash
cd d:/FlutterProjects/futuristic
flutter run
```

### 2. Switch Variants:

Edit `lib/main.dart` line 59:
```dart
bool _showVariant = false;  // First variant (Neural Network)
bool _showVariant = true;   // Second variant (Geometric)
```

### 3. Customize Splash:

Edit configuration in `main.dart`:
```dart
SplashScreen(
  config: SplashConfig(
    appName: 'YOUR APP NAME',
    tagline: 'YOUR TAGLINE',
    progressValue: 0.5,  // 50% progress
    displayDuration: Duration(seconds: 5),
  ),
  onComplete: _navigateToHome,
)
```

### 4. Control Features:

```dart
SplashConfig(
  showParticles: false,  // Disable particles
  showGlow: false,       // Disable glow effects
  logoVariant: LogoVariant.geometric,  // Use geometric logo
)
```

## ğŸ“ Navigation

Auto-navigation happens after `displayDuration`:
```dart
onComplete: () {
  // Navigate to your home screen
  Navigator.pushReplacement(
    context,
    MaterialPageRoute(builder: (_) => YourHomeScreen()),
  );
}
```

### File 18: gradlew
**Path:** `android\gradlew`
**Size:** 4.85 KB

```text
#!/usr/bin/env bash

##############################################################################
##
##  Gradle start up script for UN*X
##
##############################################################################

# Add default JVM options here. You can also use JAVA_OPTS and GRADLE_OPTS to pass JVM options to this script.
DEFAULT_JVM_OPTS=""

APP_NAME="Gradle"
APP_BASE_NAME=`basename "$0"`

# Use the maximum available, or set MAX_FD != -1 to use that value.
MAX_FD="maximum"

warn ( ) {
    echo "$*"
}

die ( ) {
    echo
    echo "$*"
    echo
    exit 1
}

# OS specific support (must be 'true' or 'false').
cygwin=false
msys=false
darwin=false
case "`uname`" in
  CYGWIN* )
    cygwin=true
    ;;
  Darwin* )
    darwin=true
    ;;
  MINGW* )
    msys=true
    ;;
esac

# Attempt to set APP_HOME
# Resolve links: $0 may be a link
PRG="$0"
# Need this for relative symlinks.
while [ -h "$PRG" ] ; do
    ls=`ls -ld "$PRG"`
    link=`expr "$ls" : '.*-> \(.*\)$'`
    if expr "$link" : '/.*' > /dev/null; then
        PRG="$link"
    else
        PRG=`dirname "$PRG"`"/$link"
    fi
done
SAVED="`pwd`"
cd "`dirname \"$PRG\"`/" >/dev/null
APP_HOME="`pwd -P`"
cd "$SAVED" >/dev/null

CLASSPATH=$APP_HOME/gradle/wrapper/gradle-wrapper.jar

# Determine the Java command to use to start the JVM.
if [ -n "$JAVA_HOME" ] ; then
    if [ -x "$JAVA_HOME/jre/sh/java" ] ; then
        # IBM's JDK on AIX uses strange locations for the executables
        JAVACMD="$JAVA_HOME/jre/sh/java"
    else
        JAVACMD="$JAVA_HOME/bin/java"
    fi
    if [ ! -x "$JAVACMD" ] ; then
        die "ERROR: JAVA_HOME is set to an invalid directory: $JAVA_HOME

Please set the JAVA_HOME variable in your environment to match the
location of your Java installation."
    fi
else
    JAVACMD="java"
    which java >/dev/null 2>&1 || die "ERROR: JAVA_HOME is not set and no 'java' command could be found in your PATH.

Please set the JAVA_HOME variable in your environment to match the
location of your Java installation."
fi

# Increase the maximum file descriptors if we can.
if [ "$cygwin" = "false" -a "$darwin" = "false" ] ; then
    MAX_FD_LIMIT=`ulimit -H -n`
    if [ $? -eq 0 ] ; then
        if [ "$MAX_FD" = "maximum" -o "$MAX_FD" = "max" ] ; then
            MAX_FD="$MAX_FD_LIMIT"
        fi
        ulimit -n $MAX_FD
        if [ $? -ne 0 ] ; then
            warn "Could not set maximum file descriptor limit: $MAX_FD"
        fi
    else
        warn "Could not query maximum file descriptor limit: $MAX_FD_LIMIT"
    fi
fi

# For Darwin, add options to specify how the application appears in the dock
if $darwin; then
    GRADLE_OPTS="$GRADLE_OPTS \"-Xdock:name=$APP_NAME\" \"-Xdock:icon=$APP_HOME/media/gradle.icns\""
fi

# For Cygwin, switch paths to Windows format before running java
if $cygwin ; then
    APP_HOME=`cygpath --path --mixed "$APP_HOME"`
    CLASSPATH=`cygpath --path --mixed "$CLASSPATH"`
    JAVACMD=`cygpath --unix "$JAVACMD"`

    # We build the pattern for arguments to be converted via cygpath
    ROOTDIRSRAW=`find -L / -maxdepth 1 -mindepth 1 -type d 2>/dev/null`
    SEP=""
    for dir in $ROOTDIRSRAW ; do
        ROOTDIRS="$ROOTDIRS$SEP$dir"
        SEP="|"
    done
    OURCYGPATTERN="(^($ROOTDIRS))"
    # Add a user-defined pattern to the cygpath arguments
    if [ "$GRADLE_CYGPATTERN" != "" ] ; then
        OURCYGPATTERN="$OURCYGPATTERN|($GRADLE_CYGPATTERN)"
    fi
    # Now convert the arguments - kludge to limit ourselves to /bin/sh
    i=0
    for arg in "$@" ; do
        CHECK=`echo "$arg"|egrep -c "$OURCYGPATTERN" -`
        CHECK2=`echo "$arg"|egrep -c "^-"`                                 ### Determine if an option

        if [ $CHECK -ne 0 ] && [ $CHECK2 -eq 0 ] ; then                    ### Added a condition
            eval `echo args$i`=`cygpath --path --ignore --mixed "$arg"`
        else
            eval `echo args$i`="\"$arg\""
        fi
        i=$((i+1))
    done
    case $i in
        (0) set -- ;;
        (1) set -- "$args0" ;;
        (2) set -- "$args0" "$args1" ;;
        (3) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" ;;
        (4) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" ;;
        (5) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" "$args4" ;;
        (6) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" "$args4" "$args5" ;;
        (7) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" "$args4" "$args5" "$args6" ;;
        (8) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" "$args4" "$args5" "$args6" "$args7" ;;
        (9) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" "$args4" "$args5" "$args6" "$args7" "$args8" ;;
    esac
fi

# Split up the JVM_OPTS And GRADLE_OPTS values into an array, following the shell quoting and substitution rules
function splitJvmOpts() {
    JVM_OPTS=("$@")
}
eval splitJvmOpts $DEFAULT_JVM_OPTS $JAVA_OPTS $GRADLE_OPTS
JVM_OPTS[${#JVM_OPTS[*]}]="-Dorg.gradle.appname=$APP_BASE_NAME"

exec "$JAVACMD" "${JVM_OPTS[@]}" -classpath "$CLASSPATH" org.gradle.wrapper.GradleWrapperMain "$@"

```

```text
@if "%DEBUG%" == "" @echo off
@rem ##########################################################################
@rem
@rem  Gradle startup script for Windows
@rem
@rem ##########################################################################

@rem Set local scope for the variables with windows NT shell
if "%OS%"=="Windows_NT" setlocal

@rem Add default JVM options here. You can also use JAVA_OPTS and GRADLE_OPTS to pass JVM options to this script.
set DEFAULT_JVM_OPTS=

set DIRNAME=%~dp0
if "%DIRNAME%" == "" set DIRNAME=.
set APP_BASE_NAME=%~n0
set APP_HOME=%DIRNAME%

@rem Find java.exe
if defined JAVA_HOME goto findJavaFromJavaHome

set JAVA_EXE=java.exe
%JAVA_EXE% -version >NUL 2>&1
if "%ERRORLEVEL%" == "0" goto init

echo.
echo ERROR: JAVA_HOME is not set and no 'java' command could be found in your PATH.
echo.
echo Please set the JAVA_HOME variable in your environment to match the
echo location of your Java installation.

goto fail

:findJavaFromJavaHome
set JAVA_HOME=%JAVA_HOME:"=%
set JAVA_EXE=%JAVA_HOME%/bin/java.exe

if exist "%JAVA_EXE%" goto init

echo.
echo ERROR: JAVA_HOME is set to an invalid directory: %JAVA_HOME%
echo.
echo Please set the JAVA_HOME variable in your environment to match the
echo location of your Java installation.

goto fail

:init
@rem Get command-line arguments, handling Windowz variants

if not "%OS%" == "Windows_NT" goto win9xME_args
if "%@eval[2+2]" == "4" goto 4NT_args

:win9xME_args
@rem Slurp the command line arguments.
set CMD_LINE_ARGS=
set _SKIP=2

:win9xME_args_slurp
if "x%~1" == "x" goto execute

set CMD_LINE_ARGS=%*
goto execute

:4NT_args
@rem Get arguments from the 4NT Shell from JP Software
set CMD_LINE_ARGS=%$

:execute
@rem Setup the command line

set CLASSPATH=%APP_HOME%\gradle\wrapper\gradle-wrapper.jar

@rem Execute Gradle
"%JAVA_EXE%" %DEFAULT_JVM_OPTS% %JAVA_OPTS% %GRADLE_OPTS% "-Dorg.gradle.appname=%APP_BASE_NAME%" -classpath "%CLASSPATH%" org.gradle.wrapper.GradleWrapperMain %CMD_LINE_ARGS%

:end
@rem End local scope for the variables with windows NT shell
if "%ERRORLEVEL%"=="0" goto mainEnd

:fail
rem Set variable GRADLE_EXIT_CONSOLE if you need the _script_ return code instead of
rem the _cmd.exe /c_ return code!
if  not "" == "%GRADLE_EXIT_CONSOLE%" exit 1
exit /b 1

:mainEnd
if "%OS%"=="Windows_NT" endlocal

:omega
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

class AIRetouchOption {
  final String id;
  final String name;
  final IconData icon;
  final Color color;
  bool isEnabled;
  double value;

  AIRetouchOption({
    required this.id,
    required this.name,
    required this.icon,
    required this.color,
    this.isEnabled = false,
    this.value = 50.0,
  });
}

// Predefined options
class AIRetouchOptions {
  static AIRetouchOption blemishRemoval = AIRetouchOption(
    id: 'blemish_removal',
    name: 'Blemish Removal',
    icon: Icons.blur_on,
    color: const Color(0xFF9333ea),
    isEnabled: true,
  );

  static AIRetouchOption eyeEnhancement = AIRetouchOption(
    id: 'eye_enhancement',
    name: 'Eye Enhancement',
    icon: Icons.visibility,
    color: const Color(0xFF0891b2),
    isEnabled: false,
  );

  static AIRetouchOption teethWhitening = AIRetouchOption(
    id: 'teeth_whitening',
    name: 'Teeth Whitening',
    icon: Icons.mood,
    color: const Color(0xFFf59e0b),
    isEnabled: false,
  );

  static AIRetouchOption skinSmoothing = AIRetouchOption(
    id: 'skin_smoothing',
    name: 'Skin Smoothing',
    icon: Icons.face,
    color: const Color(0xFFf97316),
    isEnabled: true,
    value: 75.0,
  );

  static List<AIRetouchOption> getAllOptions() {
    return [
      blemishRemoval,
      eyeEnhancement,
      teethWhitening,
      skinSmoothing,
    ];
  }
}

enum FaceShape {
  slimVLine,
  naturalOval,
  chiselled,
}

enum EditorTab {
  face,
  eyes,
  body,
  auto,
}

enum IntensityPreset {
  subtle,
  natural,
  enhanced,
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

enum EnhancementStyle {

}

class DetectedIssue {
  final String id;
  final String title;
  final String subtitle;
  final IconData icon;
  final Color iconColor;
  bool isFixed;

  DetectedIssue({
    required this.id,
    required this.title,
    required this.subtitle,
    required this.icon,
    required this.iconColor,
    this.isFixed = false,
  });
}

// Predefined enhancement styles
class EnhancementStyles {
  static const natural = EnhancementStyle.natural;
  static const glamour = EnhancementStyle.glamour;
  static const pro = EnhancementStyle.pro;

  static String getLabel(EnhancementStyle style) {
    switch (style) {
      case EnhancementStyle.natural:
        return 'NATURAL';
      case EnhancementStyle.glamour:
        return 'GLAMOUR';
      case EnhancementStyle.pro:
        return 'PRO';
    }
  }

  static IconData getIcon(EnhancementStyle style) {
    switch (style) {
      case EnhancementStyle.natural:
        return Icons.eco;
      case EnhancementStyle.glamour:
        return Icons.diamond;
      case EnhancementStyle.pro:
        return Icons.work_outline;
    }
  }
}

class DetectedIssues {
```

```dart
/// Configuration model for splash screen
class SplashConfig {
  final String appName;
  final String tagline;
  final String progressLabel;
  final double progressValue;
  final bool showParticles;
  final bool showGlow;
  final Duration displayDuration;
  final LogoVariant logoVariant;
  
  const SplashConfig({
    this.appName = 'RETOUNIQ',
    this.tagline = 'AI PHOTO ENGINE',
    this.progressLabel = 'INITIALIZING NEURAL CORE',
    this.progressValue = 0.74,
    this.showParticles = true,
    this.showGlow = true,
    this.displayDuration = const Duration(seconds: 3),
    this.logoVariant = LogoVariant.neuralNetwork,
  });
  
  SplashConfig copyWith({
    String? appName,
    String? tagline,
    String? progressLabel,
    double? progressValue,
    bool? showParticles,
    bool? showGlow,
    Duration? displayDuration,
    LogoVariant? logoVariant,
  }) {
    return SplashConfig(
      appName: appName ?? this.appName,
      tagline: tagline ?? this.tagline,
      progressLabel: progressLabel ?? this.progressLabel,
      progressValue: progressValue ?? this.progressValue,
      showParticles: showParticles ?? this.showParticles,
      showGlow: showGlow ?? this.showGlow,
      displayDuration: displayDuration ?? this.displayDuration,
      logoVariant: logoVariant ?? this.logoVariant,
    );
  }
}

/// Logo variant types
enum LogoVariant {
  neuralNetwork,  // Complex SVG with neural network paths
  geometric,      // Large R with geometric background
}

/// Particle configuration
class ParticleConfig {
  final double size;
  final double opacity;
  final double blur;
  final double top;
  final double left;
  
  const ParticleConfig({
    required this.size,
    required this.opacity,
    required this.blur,
    required this.top,
    required this.left,
  });
}
```

### File 48: ai_processing_screen.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\ai_processing_screen.dart`
**Size:** 2.95 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'dart:async';
import '../../models/ai_retouch_option.dart';
import '../../widgets/ai_retouch/processing_indicator.dart';
import '../../widgets/ai_retouch/retouch_toggle_option.dart';
import 'ai_retouch_editor_screen.dart';

class AIProcessingScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  final String imagePath;

  const AIProcessingScreen({
    super.key,
    required this.imagePath,
  });

  @override
  State<AIProcessingScreen> createState() => _AIProcessingScreenState();
}

class _AIProcessingScreenState extends State<AIProcessingScreen> {
  final List<AIRetouchOption> _options = AIRetouchOptions.getAllOptions();

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _startProcessing();
  }

  void _startProcessing() {
    // Simulate AI processing for 3 seconds
    Timer(const Duration(seconds: 3), () {
      if (mounted) {
        Navigator.of(context).pushReplacement(
          MaterialPageRoute(
            builder: (context) => AIRetouchEditorScreen(
              imagePath: widget.imagePath,
              initialOptions: _options,
            ),
          ),
        );
      }
    });
  }

  void _toggleOption(int index, bool value) {
    setState(() {
      _options[index].isEnabled = value;
    });
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: const Color(0xFF0f080c),
      body: Stack(
        children: [
          // Blurred background image
          Positioned.fill(
            child: Image.asset(
              widget.imagePath,
              fit: BoxFit.cover,
              errorBuilder: (context, error, stackTrace) {
                return Container(color: const Color(0xFF221019));
              },
            ),
          ),
          // Dark overlay
          Positioned.fill(
            child: Container(
              color: Colors.black.withValues(alpha: 0.6),
            ),
          ),
          // Processing indicator
          const Center(
            child: ProcessingIndicator(),
          ),
          // Bottom toggle options
          Positioned(
            bottom: 80,
            left: 16,
            right: 16,
            child: Column(
              mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
              children: [
                RetouchToggleOption(
                  option: _options[0],
                  onToggle: (value) => _toggleOption(0, value),
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 12),
                RetouchToggleOption(
                  option: _options[1],
                  onToggle: (value) => _toggleOption(1, value),
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 12),
                RetouchToggleOption(
                  option: _options[2],
                  onToggle: (value) => _toggleOption(2, value),
                ),
              ],
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

### File 49: ai_retouch_editor_screen.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\ai_retouch_editor_screen.dart`
**Size:** 4.14 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'dart:async';
import '../../models/ai_retouch_option.dart';
import '../../widgets/ai_retouch/editor_app_bar.dart';
import '../../widgets/ai_retouch/before_after_viewer.dart';
import '../../widgets/ai_retouch/editor_tabs.dart';
import '../../widgets/ai_retouch/slider_control.dart';
import '../../widgets/ai_retouch/face_shape_presets.dart';
import '../../widgets/ai_retouch/editor_bottom_bar.dart';
import '../../widgets/ai_retouch/ai_progress_overlay.dart';
import '../../widgets/ai_retouch/retouch_toggle_option.dart';
import '../../widgets/ai_retouch/eyes_tab_content.dart';
import '../../widgets/ai_retouch/body_tab_content.dart';
import '../../widgets/ai_retouch/auto_tab_content.dart';

class AIRetouchEditorScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  final String imagePath;
  final List<AIRetouchOption> initialOptions;

  const AIRetouchEditorScreen({
    super.key,
    required this.imagePath,
    required this.initialOptions,
  });

  @override
  State<AIRetouchEditorScreen> createState() => _AIRetouchEditorScreenState();
}

class _AIRetouchEditorScreenState extends State<AIRetouchEditorScreen> {
  EditorTab _selectedTab = EditorTab.face;
  FaceShape? _selectedFaceShape = FaceShape.slimVLine;
  double _skinSmoothness = 75.0;
  double _blemishRemovalIntensity = 50.0;
  double _aiProgress = 45.0;
  bool _showProgress = true;
  late List<AIRetouchOption> _options;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _options = widget.initialOptions;
    _simulateProgress();
  }

  void _simulateProgress() {
    Timer.periodic(const Duration(milliseconds: 100), (timer) {
      if (!mounted) {
        timer.cancel();
        return;
      }
      setState(() {
        _aiProgress += 2;
        if (_aiProgress >= 100) {
          _showProgress = false;
          timer.cancel();
        }
      });
    });
  }

  void _toggleOption(int index, bool value) {
    setState(() {
      _options[index].isEnabled = value;
    });
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: const Color(0xFF0f080c),
      appBar: const EditorAppBar(),
      body: Stack(
        children: [
          SingleChildScrollView(
            child: Column(
              children: [
                // Image viewer
                Padding(
                  padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
                  child: BeforeAfterViewer(imagePath: widget.imagePath),
                ),
                // Tabs
                EditorTabs(
                  selectedTab: _selectedTab,
                  onTabSelected: (tab) {
                    setState(() {
                      _selectedTab = tab;
                    });
                  },
                ),
                // Controls
                Padding(
                  padding: const EdgeInsets.all(24),
                  child: _buildTabContent(),
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 120),
              ],
            ),
          ),
          // Progress overlay
          if (_showProgress) AIProgressOverlay(progress: _aiProgress),
        ],
      ),
      bottomNavigationBar: const EditorBottomBar(),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildTabContent() {
    switch (_selectedTab) {
      case EditorTab.face:
        return _buildFaceTab();
      case EditorTab.eyes:
        return const EyesTabContent();
      case EditorTab.body:
        return const BodyTabContent();
      case EditorTab.auto:
        return const AutoTabContent();
    }
  }

  Widget _buildFaceTab() {
    return Column(
      children: [
        SliderControl(
          label: 'Skin Smoothness',
          value: _skinSmoothness,
          onChanged: (value) {
            setState(() {
              _skinSmoothness = value;
            });
          },
        ),
        const SizedBox(height: 32),
        FaceShapePresets(
          selectedShape: _selectedFaceShape,
          onShapeSelected: (shape) {
            setState(() {
              _selectedFaceShape = shape;
            });
          },
        ),
      ],
    );
  }
}

```

### File 50: home_screen.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\home_screen.dart`
**Size:** 4.09 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:image_picker/image_picker.dart';
import '../theme/home_theme.dart';
import '../widgets/home/home_app_bar.dart';
import '../widgets/home/upload_card.dart';
import '../widgets/home/camera_gallery_buttons.dart';
import '../widgets/home/tools_section.dart';
import '../widgets/home/recent_edits_section.dart';
import '../widgets/home/bottom_navigation.dart';
import 'ai_processing_screen.dart';
import 'remove_object_editor_screen.dart';

class HomeScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  const HomeScreen({super.key});

  @override
  State<HomeScreen> createState() => _HomeScreenState();
}

class _HomeScreenState extends State<HomeScreen> {
  int _currentNavIndex = 0;
  List<String> _recentEdits = [];

  void _handleImageSelected(XFile? image) {
    if (image != null) {
      setState(() {
        _recentEdits.insert(0, image.path);
        if (_recentEdits.length > 6) {
          _recentEdits = _recentEdits.sublist(0, 6);
        }
      });
      
      ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
        SnackBar(content: Text('Image selected: ${image.name}')),
      );
    }
  }

  void _handleNavTap(int index) {
    setState(() {
      _currentNavIndex = index;
    });
    
    final tabs = ['Home', 'Templates', 'Projects', 'Profile'];
    ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
      SnackBar(content: Text('${tabs[index]} tab selected')),
    );
  }

  void _handleSettings() {
    ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
      const SnackBar(content: Text('Settings opened')),
    );
  }

  Future<void> _handleAIRetouch() async {
    // Open gallery to select image
    final ImagePicker picker = ImagePicker();
    final XFile? image = await picker.pickImage(source: ImageSource.gallery);
    
    if (image != null && mounted) {
      // Navigate to AI Processing Screen
      Navigator.of(context).push(
        MaterialPageRoute(
          builder: (context) => AIProcessingScreen(imagePath: image.path),
        ),
      );
    }
  }

  Future<void> _handleRemoveObject() async {
    // Open gallery to select image
    final ImagePicker picker = ImagePicker();
    final XFile? image = await picker.pickImage(source: ImageSource.gallery);
    
    if (image != null && mounted) {
      // Navigate to Remove Object Editor Screen
      Navigator.of(context).push(
        MaterialPageRoute(
          builder: (context) => RemoveObjectEditorScreen(imagePath: image.path),
        ),
      );
    }
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    final isDark = Theme.of(context).brightness == Brightness.dark;
    
    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: isDark ? HomeTheme.backgroundDark : HomeTheme.backgroundLight,
      appBar: HomeAppBar(onSettings: _handleSettings),
      body: SingleChildScrollView(
        child: Column(
          crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
          children: [
            // Upload Card
            UploadCard(onImageSelected: _handleImageSelected),
            
            // Camera and Gallery Buttons
            CameraGalleryButtons(onImageSelected: _handleImageSelected),
            
            // Tools Section
            ToolsSection(
              onAIRetouch: _handleAIRetouch,
              onRemoveObject: _handleRemoveObject,
              onSeeAll: () {
                ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
                  const SnackBar(content: Text('See all tools')),
                );
              },
            ),
            
            // Recent Edits Section
            RecentEditsSection(
              recentImagePaths: _recentEdits,
              onImageTap: (path) {
                ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
                  SnackBar(content: Text('Opening image: $path')),
                );
              },
            ),
            
            const SizedBox(height: 24),
          ],
        ),
      ),
      bottomNavigationBar: BottomNavigation(
        currentIndex: _currentNavIndex,
        onTap: _handleNavTap,
      ),
    );
  }
}

```

### File 51: removal_processing_screen.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\removal_processing_screen.dart`
**Size:** 3.28 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'dart:async';
import 'removal_success_screen.dart';

class RemovalProcessingScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  final String imagePath;

  const RemovalProcessingScreen({
    super.key,
    required this.imagePath,
  });

  @override
  State<RemovalProcessingScreen> createState() => _RemovalProcessingScreenState();
}

class _RemovalProcessingScreenState extends State<RemovalProcessingScreen>
    with SingleTickerProviderStateMixin {
  late AnimationController _controller;
  double _progress = 0.0;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _controller = AnimationController(
      duration: const Duration(seconds: 3),
      vsync: this,
    )..repeat();
    
    _simulateProcessing();
  }

  void _simulateProcessing() {
    Timer.periodic(const Duration(milliseconds: 50), (timer) {
      if (mounted) {
        setState(() {
          _progress += 2;
          if (_progress >= 100) {
            timer.cancel();
            _navigateToSuccess();
          }
        });
      } else {
        timer.cancel();
      }
    });
  }

  void _navigateToSuccess() {
    Timer(const Duration(milliseconds: 500), () {
      if (mounted) {
        Navigator.of(context).pushReplacement(
          MaterialPageRoute(
            builder: (context) => RemovalSuccessScreen(imagePath: widget.imagePath),
          ),
        );
      }
    });
  }

  @override
  void dispose() {
    _controller.dispose();
    super.dispose();
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: Colors.black,
      body: Stack(
        children: [
          Positioned.fill(
            child: Opacity(
              opacity: 0.3,
              child: Image.asset(
                widget.imagePath,
                fit: BoxFit.cover,
                errorBuilder: (context, error, stackTrace) {
                  return Container(color: Colors.black);
                },
              ),
            ),
          ),
          Center(
            child: Column(
              mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
              children: [
                SizedBox(
                  width: 80,
                  height: 80,
                  child: Stack(
                    alignment: Alignment.center,
                    children: [
                      RotationTransition(
                        turns: _controller,
                        child: Container(
                          width: 80,
                          height: 80,
                          decoration: const BoxDecoration(
                            shape: BoxShape.circle,
                            gradient: SweepGradient(
                              colors: [
                                Color(0xFFf20d80),
                                Color(0xFF9c27b0),
                                Color(0xFF00f2ff),
                              Color(0xFFf20d80),
                              ],
                            ),
                          ),
                        ),
                      ),
                    ],
                  ),
                ),
              ],
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}

```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

class RemovalSuccessScreen extends StatelessWidget {
  final String imagePath;

  const RemovalSuccessScreen({super.key, required this.imagePath});

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      body: Container(
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          gradient: RadialGradient(
            center: Alignment.topCenter,
            colors: [
              const Color(0xFF1a0b2e),
              Colors.black,
            ],
          ),
        ),
        child: Column(
          children: [
            _buildHeader(context),
            Expanded(child: _buildContent(context)),
            _buildActions(context),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildHeader(BuildContext context) {
    return Padding(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.only(top: 48, left: 24, right: 24, bottom: 16),
      child: Row(
        mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
        children: [
          IconButton(
            onPressed: () => Navigator.of(context).pop(),
            icon: const Icon(Icons.close, color: Colors.white),
          ),
          Text(
            'RETOUNIQ',
            style: TextStyle(
              color: Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.4),
              fontSize: 10,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
              letterSpacing: 3,
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(width: 48),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildContent(BuildContext context) {
    return SingleChildScrollView(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(24),
      child: Column(
        children: [
          // Success icon
          Container(
            width: 80,
            height: 80,
            decoration: BoxDecoration(
              shape: BoxShape.circle,
              gradient: const LinearGradient(
                colors: [Color(0xFFf20d80), Color(0xFF9c27b0)],
              ),
              boxShadow: [
                BoxShadow(
                  color: const Color(0xFFf20d80).withValues(alpha: 0.3),
                  blurRadius: 30,
                ),
              ],
            ),
            child: const Icon(
              Icons.check_circle,
              color: Color(0xFF4ade80),
              size: 40,
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 16),
          const Text(
            'Success!',
            style: TextStyle(
              color: Colors.white,
              fontSize: 24,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 4),
          Text(
            'Photo ready for export',
            style: TextStyle(
              color: Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.4),
              fontSize: 12,
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 40),
          // Preview
          ClipRRect(
            borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(24),
            child: Image.asset(
              imagePath,
              width: MediaQuery.of(context).size.width * 0.8,
              fit: BoxFit.contain,
              errorBuilder: (context, error, stackTrace) {
                return Container(
                  height: 400,
                  color: Colors.grey[900],
                  child: const Center(
                    child: Icon(Icons.image, color: Colors.white54, size:64),
                  ),
                );
              },
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );

  Widget _buildActions(BuildContext context) {

              // TODO: Implement save

                const SnackBar(content: Text('Saved to gallery!')),
              );
            },
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 12),
          // Share button
          _ActionButton(
            label: 'SHARE TO SOCIALS',
            icon: Icons.ios_share,
            onTap: () {
              // TODO: Implement share
            },
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}

class _ActionButton extends StatelessWidget {
  final String label;
  final IconData icon;
  final bool gradient;
  final VoidCallback? onTap;

  const _ActionButton({
    required this.label,
    required this.icon,
    this.gradient = false,
    this.onTap,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return GestureDetector(
      onTap: onTap,
      child: Container(
        width: double.infinity,
        padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 20),
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          gradient: gradient
              ? const LinearGradient(
                  colors: [Color(0xFFf20d80), Color(0xFF9c27b0)],
                )
              : null,
          color: gradient ? null : Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.05),
          border: gradient ? null : Border.all(color: Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.1)),
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16),
          boxShadow: gradient
              ? [
                  BoxShadow(
                    color: const Color(0xFFf20d80).withValues(alpha: 0.2),
                    blurRadius: 20,
                  ),
                ]
              : null,
        ),
        child: Row(
          mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
          children: [
            Text(
              label,
              style: const TextStyle(
                color: Colors.white,
                fontSize: 14,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                letterSpacing: 1.5,
              ),
            ),
            const SizedBox(width: 8),
            Icon(icon, color: Colors.white, size: 20),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

### File 53: remove_object_editor_screen.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\remove_object_editor_screen.dart`
**Size:** 2.65 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../models/removal_tool_model.dart';
import '../widgets/remove_object/removal_editor_header.dart';
import '../widgets/remove_object/removal_toolbar.dart';
import '../widgets/remove_object/removal_action_buttons.dart';
import 'removal_processing_screen.dart';

class RemoveObjectEditorScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  final String imagePath;

  const RemoveObjectEditorScreen({super.key, required this.imagePath});

  @override
  State<RemoveObjectEditorScreen> createState() => _RemoveObjectEditorScreenState();
}

class _RemoveObjectEditorScreenState extends State<RemoveObjectEditorScreen> {
  RemovalTool _selectedTool = RemovalTool.brush;
  double _brushSize = 35.0;
  final List<BrushPoint> _brushStrokes = [];
  bool _canUndo = false;
  bool _canRedo = false;

  void _handleRemove() {
    _brushStrokes.add(BrushPoint(const Offset(100, 100), _brushSize));
    Navigator.of(context).push(
      MaterialPageRoute(
        builder: (context) => RemovalProcessingScreen(imagePath: widget.imagePath),
      ),
    );
  }

  void _clearAll() {
    setState(() {
      _brushStrokes.clear();
      _canUndo = false;
      _canRedo = false;
    });
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: Colors.black,
      body: Stack(
        children: [
          Column(
            children: [
              RemovalEditorHeader(
                canUndo: _canUndo,
                canRedo: _canRedo,
                onBack: () => Navigator.of(context).pop(),
              ),
              Expanded(
                child: Center(
                  child: Image.asset(
                    widget.imagePath,
                    fit: BoxFit.contain,
                    errorBuilder: (context, error, stackTrace) {
                      return Container(
                        color: Colors.grey[900],
                        child: const Center(
                          child: Icon(Icons.image, color: Colors.white54, size: 64),
                        ),
                      );
                    },
                  ),
                ),
              ),
              RemovalToolbar(
                selectedTool: _selectedTool,
                brushSize: _brushSize,
                onToolChanged: (tool) => setState(() => _selectedTool = tool),
                onBrushSizeChanged: (size) => setState(() => _brushSize = size),
              ),
            ],
          ),
          RemovalActionButtons(
            onClearAll: _clearAll,
            onRemove: _handleRemove,
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

### File 54: splash_screen.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\splash_screen.dart`
**Size:** 4.75 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../config/app_config.dart';
import '../models/splash_config.dart';
import '../widgets/splash/animated_particles.dart';
import '../widgets/splash/logo_variants.dart';
import '../widgets/splash/progress_bar.dart';
import '../widgets/splash/bottom_glow.dart';

/// Main splash screen with neural network logo variant
class SplashScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  final SplashConfig config;
  final VoidCallback? onComplete;
  
  const SplashScreen({
    super.key,
    this.config = const SplashConfig(),
    this.onComplete,
  });
  
  @override
  State<SplashScreen> createState() => _SplashScreenState();
}

class _SplashScreenState extends State<SplashScreen>
    with SingleTickerProviderStateMixin {
  late AnimationController _progressController;
  late Animation<double> _progressAnimation;
  
  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    
    // Setup progress animation from 0.01 (1%) to 1.0 (100%)
    _progressController = AnimationController(
      vsync: this,
      duration: widget.config.displayDuration,
    );
    
    _progressAnimation = Tween<double>(
      begin: 0.01,
      end: 1.0,
    ).animate(CurvedAnimation(
      parent: _progressController,
      curve: Curves.easeInOut,
    ));
    
    // Start animation
    _progressController.forward();
    
    // Auto-navigate after duration
    Future.delayed(widget.config.displayDuration, () {
      if (mounted && widget.onComplete != null) {
        widget.onComplete!();
      }
    });
  }
  
  @override
  void dispose() {
    _progressController.dispose();
    super.dispose();
  }
  
  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: AppConfig.backgroundDark,
      body: Container(
        decoration: const BoxDecoration(
          gradient: LinearGradient(
            begin: Alignment.topCenter,
            end: Alignment.bottomCenter,
            colors: [
              Colors.black,
              Color(0xFF0a0508),
              Color(0xFF221019),
            ],
          ),
        ),
        child: Stack(
          children: [
            // Animated particles
            AnimatedParticles(enabled: widget.config.showParticles),
            
            // Main content
            SafeArea(
              child: Padding(
                padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(
                  horizontal: AppConfig.defaultPadding * 1.5,
                  vertical: AppConfig.defaultPadding,
                ),
                child: Column(
                  children: [
                    const SafeAreaSpacer(height: 40),
                    
                    // Central logo section
                    Expanded(
                      child: Center(
                        child: Column(
                          mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
                          children: [
                            LogoWidget(
                              variant: widget.config.logoVariant,
                              showGlow: widget.config.showGlow,
                            ),
                            const SizedBox(height: 32),
                            Text(
                              widget.config.appName,
                              style: AppConfig.headlineStyle,
                            ),
                            const SizedBox(height: 12),
                            Text(
                              widget.config.tagline,
                              style: AppConfig.subtitleStyle,
                            ),
                          ],
                        ),
                      ),
                    ),
                    
                    // Bottom progress section
                    SizedBox(
                      width: double.infinity,
                      child: Column(
                        children: [
                          AnimatedBuilder(
                            animation: _progressAnimation,
                            builder: (context, child) {
                              return ProgressBar(
                                label: widget.config.progressLabel,
                                progress: _progressAnimation.value,
                              );
                            },
                          ),
                          const SizedBox(height: 24),
                          const PoweredByFooter(),
                        ],
                      ),
                    ),
                    
                    const BottomSpacer(height: 32),
                  ],
                ),
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
class _SplashVariantScreenState extends State<SplashVariantScreen>
    with SingleTickerProviderStateMixin {
  late AnimationController _progressController;
  late Animation<double> _progressAnimation;

  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    
    // Setup progress animation from 0.01 (1%) to 1.0 (100%)
    _progressController = AnimationController(
      vsync: this,
      duration: widget.config.displayDuration,
    );
    
    _progressAnimation = Tween<double>(
      begin: 0.01,
      end: 1.0,
    ).animate(CurvedAnimation(
      parent: _progressController,
      curve: Curves.easeInOut,
    ));

    _progressController.forward();

      if (mounted && widget.onComplete != null) {
        widget.onComplete!();
      }
    });
  }
  
  @override

    _progressController.dispose();
    super.dispose();
  }
  
  @override

    return Scaffold(
```

### File 58: auto_tab_content.dart
**Path:** `lib\widgets\ai_retouch\auto_tab_content.dart`
**Size:** 5.52 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'dart:async';
import '../../models/auto_enhancement_model.dart';
import '../ai_retouch/enhance_button.dart';
import '../ai_retouch/enhancement_style_card.dart';
import '../ai_retouch/detected_issue_item.dart';

class AutoTabContent extends StatefulWidget {
  const AutoTabContent({super.key});

  @override
  State<AutoTabContent> createState() => _AutoTabContentState();
}

class _AutoTabContentState extends State<AutoTabContent> {
  EnhancementStyle _selectedStyle = EnhancementStyle.natural;
  List<DetectedIssue> _detectedIssues = [];
  bool _isEnhancing = false;
  bool _isEnhanced = false;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _detectedIssues = DetectedIssues.getIssues();
  }

  void _handleEnhance() {
    setState(() {
      _isEnhancing = true;
    });

    // Simulate AI enhancement
    Timer(const Duration(seconds: 2), () {
      if (mounted) {
        setState(() {
          _isEnhancing = false;
          _isEnhanced = true;
          // Mark all issues as fixed
          for (var issue in _detectedIssues) {
            issue.isFixed = true;
          }
        });
      }
    });
  }

  void _handleFixIssue(int index) {
    setState(() {
      _detectedIssues[index].isFixed = true;
    });
  }

  int get _fixedCount => _detectedIssues.where((i) => i.isFixed).length;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return SingleChildScrollView(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
      child: Column(
        crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
        children: [
          // Enhance button card
          Container(
            padding: const EdgeInsets.all(32),
            decoration: BoxDecoration(
              color: const Color(0xFF1a0d15).withValues(alpha: 0.6),
              borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16),
              border: Border.all(
                color: Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.1),
              ),
            ),
            child: Center(
              child: EnhanceButton(
                onEnhance: _handleEnhance,
                isProcessing: _isEnhancing,
              ),
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 24),
          
          // Enhancement style section
          Text(
            'ENHANCEMENT STYLE',
            style: TextStyle(
              color: Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.9),
              fontSize: 11,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
              letterSpacing: 2,
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 12),
          Row(
            children: [
              Expanded(
                child: EnhancementStyleCard(
                  style: EnhancementStyle.natural,
                  isSelected: _selectedStyle == EnhancementStyle.natural,
                  onTap: () => setState(() => _selectedStyle = EnhancementStyle.natural),
                ),
              ),
              const SizedBox(width: 12),
              Expanded(
                child: EnhancementStyleCard(
                  style: EnhancementStyle.glamour,
                  isSelected: _selectedStyle == EnhancementStyle.glamour,
                  onTap: () => setState(() => _selectedStyle = EnhancementStyle.glamour),
                ),
              ),
              const SizedBox(width: 12),
              Expanded(
                child: EnhancementStyleCard(
                  style: EnhancementStyle.pro,
                  isSelected: _selectedStyle == EnhancementStyle.pro,
                  onTap: () => setState(() => _selectedStyle = EnhancementStyle.pro),
                ),
              ),
            ],
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 24),
          
          // Detected issues section
          Row(
            mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
            children: [
              Text(
                'DETECTED ISSUES',
                style: TextStyle(
                  color: Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.9),
                  fontSize: 11,
                  fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                  letterSpacing: 2,
                ),
              ),
              Container(
                padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 8, vertical: 4),
                decoration: BoxDecoration(
                  color: const Color(0xFF00f2ff).withValues(alpha: 0.1),
                  borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(4),
                  border: Border.all(
                    color: const Color(0xFF00f2ff).withValues(alpha: 0.2),
                  ),
                ),
                child: Text(
                  '$_fixedCount/${_detectedIssues.length} FIXED',
                  style: const TextStyle(
                    color: Color(0xFF00f2ff),
                    fontSize: 9,
                    fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                  ),
                ),
              ),
            ],
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 12),
          ListView.separated(
            shrinkWrap: true,
            physics: const NeverScrollableScrollPhysics(),
            itemCount: _detectedIssues.length,
            separatorBuilder: (context, index) => const SizedBox(height: 8),
            itemBuilder: (context, index) {
              return DetectedIssueItem(
                issue: _detectedIssues[index],
                onFix: () => _handleFixIssue(index),
              );
            },
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'dart:io';

class BeforeAfterViewer extends StatefulWidget {
  final String imagePath;

  const BeforeAfterViewer({
    super.key,
    required this.imagePath,
  });

  @override
  State<BeforeAfterViewer> createState() => _BeforeAfterViewerState();
}

class _BeforeAfterViewerState extends State<BeforeAfterViewer> {
  double _sliderPosition = 0.5;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return AspectRatio(
      aspectRatio: 3 / 4,
      child: ClipRRect(
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(24),
        child: Stack(
          children: [
            // Background image (After)
            Positioned.fill(
              child: Image.file(
                File(widget.imagePath),
                fit: BoxFit.cover,
                errorBuilder: (context, error, stackTrace) {
                  return Container(
                    color: Colors.grey.shade800,
                    child: const Icon(Icons.image, size: 64, color: Colors.white54),
                  );
                },
              ),
            ),
            // Slider line
            Positioned(
              left: MediaQuery.of(context).size.width * _sliderPosition - 20,
              top: 0,
              bottom: 0,
              child: Container(
                width: 2,
                decoration: BoxDecoration(
                  gradient: LinearGradient(
                    begin: Alignment.topCenter,
                    end: Alignment.bottomCenter,
                    colors: [
                      Colors.transparent,
                      const Color(0xFFf20d80).withValues(alpha: 0.5),
                      Colors.transparent,
                    ],
                  ),
                ),
              ),
            ),
            // Slider handle
            Positioned(
              left: MediaQuery.of(context).size.width * _sliderPosition - 36,
              top: 0,
              bottom: 0,
              child: Center(
                child: GestureDetector(
                  onHorizontalDragUpdate: (details) {
                    setState(() {
                      _sliderPosition = (details.globalPosition.dx / 
                          MediaQuery.of(context).size.width).clamp(0.0, 1.0);
                    });
                  },
                  child: Container(
                    width: 32,
                    height: 48,
                    decoration: BoxDecoration(
                      gradient: const LinearGradient(
                        colors: [Color(0xFFf20d80), Color(0xFF9c27b0)],
                      ),
                      borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(24),
                      border: Border.all(color: Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.3), width: 2),
                      boxShadow: [
                        BoxShadow(
                          color: const Color(0xFFf20d80).withValues(alpha: 0.6),
                          blurRadius: 15,
                        ),
                      ],
                    ),
                    child: const Column(
                      mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
                      children: [
                        Icon(Icons.chevron_left, color: Colors.white, size: 12),
                        Icon(Icons.chevron_right, color: Colors.white, size: 12),
                      ],
                    ),
                  ),
                ),
              ),
            ),
            // Labels
            const Positioned(
              top: 16,
              left: 16,
              child: _Label(text: 'BEFORE', isPrimary: false),
            ),
            const Positioned(
              top: 16,
              right: 16,
              child: _Label(text: 'AFTER', isPrimary: true),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}

class _Label extends StatelessWidget {
  final String text;
  final bool isPrimary;

  const _Label({required this.text, required this.isPrimary});

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 10, vertical: 4),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: isPrimary
            ? const Color(0xFFf20d80).withValues(alpha: 0.4)
            : Colors.black.withValues(alpha: 0.4),
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(6),
      ),
      child: Text(
        text,
        style: TextStyle(
          color: isPrimary ? Colors.white : Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.6),
          fontSize: 10,
          fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
          letterSpacing: 1.5,
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
class BodyTabContent extends StatefulWidget {

class _BodyTabContentState extends State<BodyTabContent> {
  double _bodyShape = -15.0;
  double _height = 45.0;
  PosturePreset _posturePreset = PosturePreset.subtle;
  double _waist = -40.0;
  double _curves = 12.0;
  bool _showAdvancedOptions = false;

  void _resetAll() {
    setState(() {
      _bodyShape = 0.0;
      _height = 50.0;
      _posturePreset = PosturePreset.off;
      _waist = 0.0;
      _curves = 0.0;
    });

  @override

      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16),

              value: _bodyShape,
              onChanged: (value) => setState(() => _bodyShape = value),
            ),

                      child: PosturePresets(
                        selectedPreset: _posturePreset,
                        onPresetSelected: (preset) {
                          setState(() => _posturePreset = preset);
                        },
                      ),
                    ),
                  ],
                ),
              ],
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 16),

          _Card(
            child: Column(
              crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
              children: [
                Text(
                  'WAIST & CURVES',
                  style: TextStyle(
                    color: Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.9),
                    fontSize: 12,
                    fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                    letterSpacing: 2,
                  ),

                  gradientColor: const Color(0xFFf20d80),

                const SizedBox(height: 32),

                ),

          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 24),
```

### File 61: center_position_slider.dart
**Path:** `lib\widgets\ai_retouch\center_position_slider.dart`
**Size:** 4.38 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

class CenterPositionSlider extends StatelessWidget {
  final String label;
  final double value;
  final double minValue;
  final double maxValue;
  final Color gradientColor;
  final ValueChanged<double>? onChanged;

  const CenterPositionSlider({
    super.key,
    required this.label,
    required this.value,
    this.minValue = -50.0,
    this.maxValue = 50.0,
    required this.gradientColor,
    this.onChanged,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    final percentage = value.toInt();
    
    return Column(
      children: [
        // Header
        Row(
          mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
          children: [
            Text(
              label.toUpperCase(),
              style: TextStyle(
                color: Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.7),
                fontSize: 11,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                letterSpacing: 1,
              ),
            ),
            Text(
              '${percentage > 0 ? '+' : ''}$percentage%',
              style: const TextStyle(
                color: Color(0xFF00f2ff),
                fontSize: 11,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
        const SizedBox(height: 16),
        // Slider
        SizedBox(
          height: 24,
          child: Stack(
            alignment: Alignment.center,
            children: [
              // Track
              Container(
                height: 6,
                decoration: BoxDecoration(
                  color: Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.1),
                  borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(3),
                ),
              ),
              // Gradient fill (left or right from center)
              if (value < 0)
                Positioned(
                  left: 0,
                  right: MediaQuery.of(context).size.width / 2,
                  child: Container(
                    height: 6,
                    decoration: BoxDecoration(
                      gradient: LinearGradient(
                        colors: [
                          gradientColor.withValues(alpha: 0.6),
                          Colors.transparent,
                        ],
                      ),
                      borderRadius: const BorderRadius.only(
                        topLeft: Radius.circular(3),
                        bottomLeft: Radius.circular(3),
                      ),
                    ),
                  ),
                )
              else if (value > 0)
                Positioned(
                  left: MediaQuery.of(context).size.width / 2,
                  right: 0,
                  child: Container(
                    height: 6,
                    decoration: BoxDecoration(
                      gradient: LinearGradient(
                        colors: [
                          Colors.transparent,
                          gradientColor.withValues(alpha: 0.6),
                        ],
                      ),
                      borderRadius: const BorderRadius.only(
                        topRight: Radius.circular(3),
                        bottomRight: Radius.circular(3),
                      ),
                    ),
                  ),
                ),
              // Center marker
              Container(
                width: 2,
                height: 12,
                color: Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.3),
              ),
              // Thumb
              Positioned(
                left: (MediaQuery.of(context).size.width - 48) * 
                    ((value - minValue) / (maxValue - minValue)) - 10,
                child: Container(
                  width: 20,
                  height: 20,
                  decoration: BoxDecoration(
                    color: Colors.white,
                    shape: BoxShape.circle,
                    border: Border.all(color: gradientColor, width: 2),
                    boxShadow: [
                      BoxShadow(
                        color: Colors.black.withValues(alpha: 0.3),
                        blurRadius: 8,
                      ),
                    ],
                  ),
                ),
              ),
            ],
          ),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }
}

```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../models/auto_enhancement_model.dart';

class DetectedIssueItem extends StatelessWidget {
  final DetectedIssue issue;
  final VoidCallback? onFix;

  const DetectedIssueItem({
    super.key,
    required this.issue,
    this.onFix,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.05),
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
        border: Border.all(
          color: Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.05),
        ),
      ),
      child: Row(
        children: [
          // Icon
          Container(
            width: 32,
            height: 32,
            decoration: BoxDecoration(
              color: issue.iconColor.withValues(alpha: 0.1),
              borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(8),
            ),
            child: Icon(
              issue.icon,
              color: issue.iconColor,
              size: 18,
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(width: 12),
          // Text
          Expanded(
            child: Column(
              crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
              children: [
                Text(
                  issue.title,
                  style: TextStyle(
                    color: Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.9),
                    fontSize: 12,
                    fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                  ),
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 2),
                Text(
                  issue.subtitle,
                  style: TextStyle(
                    color: Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.4),
                    fontSize: 9,
                    fontWeight: FontWeight.w500,
                    letterSpacing: 1,
                  ),
                ),
              ],
            ),
          ),
          // Fix button
          GestureDetector(
            onTap: issue.isFixed ? null : onFix,
            child: Container(
              padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 20, vertical: 8),
              decoration: BoxDecoration(
                gradient: issue.isFixed
                    ? null
                    : const LinearGradient(
                        colors: [Color(0xFFf20d80), Color(0xFF9c27b0)],
                      ),
                color: issue.isFixed ? Colors.green.withValues(alpha: 0.2) : null,
                borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(20),
                boxShadow: issue.isFixed
                    ? null
                    : [
                        BoxShadow(
                          color: const Color(0xFFf20d80).withValues(alpha: 0.3),
                          blurRadius: 10,
                        ),
                      ],
              ),
              child: Text(
                issue.isFixed ? 'FIXED' : 'FIX',
                style: TextStyle(
                  color: issue.isFixed ? Colors.green : Colors.white,
                  fontSize: 10,
                  fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                  letterSpacing: 1.5,
                ),
              ),
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
class EditorAppBar extends StatelessWidget implements PreferredSizeWidget {
```

```dart
class _ActionButton extends StatelessWidget {
  final IconData icon;
  final String label;
  final VoidCallback onTap;

  const _ActionButton({
    required this.icon,
    required this.label,
    required this.onTap,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return GestureDetector(
      onTap: onTap,
      child: Padding(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.all(12),
        child: Column(
          mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
          children: [
            Icon(icon, color: Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.6), size: 24),
            const SizedBox(height: 4),
            Text(
              label,
              style: TextStyle(
                color: Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.6),
                fontSize: 9,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                letterSpacing: 1.5,
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}

class _IconButton extends StatelessWidget {
  final IconData icon;
  final VoidCallback onTap;

  const _IconButton({
    required this.icon,
    required this.onTap,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return IconButton(
      onPressed: onTap,
      icon: Icon(
        icon,
        color: Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.6),
      ),
    );
  }
```

```dart
class EditorTabs extends StatelessWidget {

class _TabItem extends StatelessWidget {

  final String label;
  final bool isSelected;
  final VoidCallback? onTap;

  const _TabItem({
    required this.icon,
    required this.label,
    required this.isSelected,
    this.onTap,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return GestureDetector(
      onTap: onTap,
      child: Container(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 12, horizontal: 16),
        decoration: BoxDecoration(

                  bottom: BorderSide(
                    width: 3,

          mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,

              icon,

              size: 24,
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 4),
            Text(
              label,
              style: TextStyle(
                color: isSelected ? const Color(0xFFf20d80) : Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.4),

                fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                letterSpacing: 1,
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

class EnhanceButton extends StatefulWidget {
  final VoidCallback? onEnhance;
  final bool isProcessing;

  const EnhanceButton({
    super.key,
    this.onEnhance,
    this.isProcessing = false,
  });

  @override
  State<EnhanceButton> createState() => _EnhanceButtonState();
}

class _EnhanceButtonState extends State<EnhanceButton>
    with SingleTickerProviderStateMixin {
  late AnimationController _controller;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _controller = AnimationController(
      duration: const Duration(seconds: 2),
      vsync: this,
    )..repeat();
  }

  @override
  void dispose() {
    _controller.dispose();
    super.dispose();
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Column(
      children: [
        // Animated enhance button
        GestureDetector(
          onTap: widget.isProcessing ? null : widget.onEnhance,
          child: AnimatedBuilder(
            animation: _controller,
            builder: (context, child) {
              return Container(
                width: 128,
                height: 128,
                decoration: BoxDecoration(
                  shape: BoxShape.circle,
                  gradient: const LinearGradient(
                    colors: [Color(0xFFf20d80), Color(0xFF9c27b0)],
                  ),
                  boxShadow: [
                    BoxShadow(
                      color: const Color(0xFFf20d80).withOpacity(
                        0.3 + (_controller.value * 0.2),
                      ),
                      blurRadius: 30,
                      spreadRadius: _controller.value * 5,
                    ),
                  ],
                ),
                child: Column(
                  mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
                  children: [
                    Icon(
                      widget.isProcessing ? Icons.hourglass_empty : Icons.auto_awesome,
                      color: Colors.white,
                      size: 40,
                    ),
                    const SizedBox(height: 4),
                    Text(
                      widget.isProcessing ? 'PROCESSING...' : 'ENHANCE NOW',
                      style: const TextStyle(
                        color: Colors.white,
                        fontSize: 10,
                        fontWeight: FontWeight.w900,
                        letterSpacing: 2,
                      ),
                    ),
                  ],
                ),
              );
            },
          ),
        ),
        const SizedBox(height: 16),
        // Subtitle
        Text(
          widget.isProcessing
              ? 'AI is working its magic...'
              : 'Tap to unleash AI perfection',
          style: TextStyle(
            color: Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.5),
            fontSize: 11,
            fontStyle: FontStyle.italic,
            letterSpacing: 1.5,
          ),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../models/eye_controls_model.dart';
import '../ai_retouch/slider_control.dart';
import '../ai_retouch/eye_toggle_control.dart';
import '../ai_retouch/eye_size_control.dart';

class EyesTabContent extends StatefulWidget {
  const EyesTabContent({super.key});

  @override
  State<EyesTabContent> createState() => _EyesTabContentState();
}

class _EyesTabContentState extends State<EyesTabContent> {
  double _eyeBrightness = 60.0;
  bool _darkCircleRemovalEnabled = true;
  double _darkCircleIntensity = 40.0;
  double _eyeSize = 0.0;
  bool _redEyeRemovalEnabled = true;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Padding(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(24),
      child: Column(
        children: [
          // Eye Brightness
          SliderControl(
            label: 'Eye Brightness',
            value: _eyeBrightness,
            accentColor: const Color(0xFFf20d80),
            onChanged: (value) {
              setState(() {
                _eyeBrightness = value;
              });
            },
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 24),
          
          // Remove Dark Circles
          EyeToggleControl(
            label: 'Remove Dark Circles',
            isEnabled: _darkCircleRemovalEnabled,
            gradientColor: const Color(0xFF9c27b0),
            intensity: _darkCircleIntensity,
            onToggle: (value) {
              setState(() {
                _darkCircleRemovalEnabled = value;
              });
            },
            onIntensityChanged: (value) {
              setState(() {
                _darkCircleIntensity = value;
              });
            },
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 24),
          
          // Eye Size
          EyeSizeControl(
            value: _eyeSize,
            onChanged: (value) {
              setState(() {
                _eyeSize = value;
              });
            },
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 24),
          
          // Red-Eye Removal
          EyeToggleControl(
            label: 'Red-Eye Removal',
            isEnabled: _redEyeRemovalEnabled,
            gradientColor: const Color(0xFF00f2ff),
            onToggle: (value) {
              setState(() {
                _redEyeRemovalEnabled = value;
              });
            },
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
class EyeSizeControl extends StatelessWidget {

                value: value,
                minValue: -20.0,
                maxValue: 20.0,
                onChanged: onChanged,
              ),
            ),

            Icon(

              size: 16,

          ),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }

class _CenterPositionSlider extends StatelessWidget {
  final double value;
  final double minValue;
  final double maxValue;
  final ValueChanged<double>? onChanged;

  const _CenterPositionSlider({
    required this.value,
    required this.minValue,
    required this.maxValue,
    this.onChanged,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    final normalizedValue = (value - minValue) / (maxValue - minValue);
    
    return SizedBox(
      height: 24,
      child: Stack(
        alignment: Alignment.center,
        children: [
          // Track
          Container(
            height: 6,
            decoration: BoxDecoration(
              color: Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.1),
              borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(3),
            ),
          ),
          // Center marker
          Container(
            width: 2,
            height: 12,
            color: Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.4),
          ),
          // Thumb
          Positioned(
            left: (MediaQuery.of(context).size.width - 80) * normalizedValue - 12,
            child: Container(
              width: 24,
              height: 24,
              decoration: BoxDecoration(
                color: Colors.white,
                shape: BoxShape.circle,
                border: Border.all(
                  color: const Color(0xFFf20d80).withValues(alpha: 0.5),
                  width: 2,
                ),
                boxShadow: [
                  BoxShadow(
                    color: Colors.black.withValues(alpha: 0.3),
                    blurRadius: 8,
                  ),
                ],
              ),
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

class EyeToggleControl extends StatelessWidget {
  final String label;
  final bool isEnabled;
  final Color gradientColor;
  final ValueChanged<bool>? onToggle;
  final double? intensity;
  final ValueChanged<double>? onIntensityChanged;

  const EyeToggleControl({
    super.key,
    required this.label,
    required this.isEnabled,
    required this.gradientColor,
    this.onToggle,
    this.intensity,
    this.onIntensityChanged,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Column(
      crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
      children: [
        // Toggle row
        Row(
          mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
          children: [
            Text(
              label,
              style: const TextStyle(
                color: Colors.white,
                fontSize: 14,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
              ),
            ),
            GestureDetector(
              onTap: () => onToggle?.call(!isEnabled),
              child: Container(
                width: 40,
                height: 20,
                decoration: BoxDecoration(
                  gradient: isEnabled
                      ? LinearGradient(colors: [gradientColor, gradientColor.withValues(alpha: 0.7)])
                      : null,
                  color: isEnabled ? null : Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.2),
                  borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(10),
                  boxShadow: isEnabled
                      ? [
                          BoxShadow(
                            color: gradientColor.withValues(alpha: 0.3),
                            blurRadius: 8,
                          ),
                        ]
                      : null,
                ),
                padding: const EdgeInsets.all(2),
                child: AnimatedAlign(
                  alignment: isEnabled ? Alignment.centerRight : Alignment.centerLeft,
                  duration: const Duration(milliseconds: 200),
                  child: Container(
                    width: 16,
                    height: 16,
                    decoration: const BoxDecoration(
                      color: Colors.white,
                      shape: BoxShape.circle,
                    ),
                  ),
                ),
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
        // Intensity slider (if provided)
        if (intensity != null && onIntensityChanged != null && isEnabled) ...[
          const SizedBox(height: 16),
          _IntensitySlider(
            value: intensity!,
            onChanged: onIntensityChanged!,
          ),
        ],
      ],
    );
  }
}

class _IntensitySlider extends StatelessWidget {
  final double value;
  final ValueChanged<double> onChanged;

  const _IntensitySlider({
    required this.value,
    required this.onChanged,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return SizedBox(
      height: 24,
      child: Stack(
        alignment: Alignment.centerLeft,
        children: [
          Container(
            height: 4,
            decoration: BoxDecoration(
              color: Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.1),
              borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(2),
            ),
          ),
          FractionallySizedBox(
            widthFactor: value / 100,
            child: Container(
              height: 4,
              decoration: BoxDecoration(
                color: Colors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.3),
                borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(2),
              ),
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}
```
